[sqrt(1+1/(c^2*x^2))/sqrt(1-c^4*x^4),x,5,-arctanh(sqrt(1-c^4*x^4)/(c*x*sqrt(1+1/(c^2*x^2))))/c,-x*arctanh(sqrt(1-c^2*x^2))*sqrt(1+1/(c^2*x^2))/sqrt(1+c^2*x^2)]]:
